</p>

***landtong.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:landtong.html>landtong</a> (91363)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tong.html>tong</a></i>. Cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Landzunge</i>, which also dates from the eighteenth century.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>spit of <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, headland <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> (200)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lanc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*langaz</i>.
</p>

</p>

<li>long (time), lengthy, a long time

***langdradig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:langdradig.html>langdradig</a> (42033)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:draad.html>draad</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:langdradig.html>langdradig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:langdradig.html>langdradiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">langdradigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>longwinded, wordy, prolix <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> consisting of long thread, long threads or other long fibres <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*langon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*langijaną</i>.

<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:langs.html>langs</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stands.html>stands</a> <b>along</b> the wall.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>past</li>
<li>through
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belangrijkste.html>belangrijkste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:centra.html>centra</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhandeling.html>verhandeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>diamant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:londen.html>Londen</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Beers <a href = vnd.unilang:gevestigd.html>gevestigd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:antwerpen.html>Antwerpen</a> (80% <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruwe.html>ruwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diamanten.html>diamanten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:langs.html>langs</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:antwerpen.html>Antwerpen</a>).</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/DiamantGeschiedenis">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>The most important centers for the handling of <a href = vnd.unilang:diamonds.html>diamonds</a> are London (where <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Beers <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> headquartered) and Antwerp (80% of all rough <a href = vnd.unilang:diamonds.html>diamonds</a> go <b>through</b> Antwerp).</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lapje.html>lapje</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kat.html>kat</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lappen.html>lappen</a> (9499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lappen.html>lappen</a></i>. <ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to piece up, to patch, to repair</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to raise (money)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay up, to put in <a href = vnd.unilang:extra.html>extra</a> money</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to clean with a shammy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play (a trick) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with indirect object</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***lappendeken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lappendeken.html>lappendeken</a> (64288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lap</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rags.html>rags</a>, pieces of cloth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deken.html>deken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blanket</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lappendeken.html>lappendeken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lappendeken.html>lappendekens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lappendeken.html>lappendekentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A blanket made of many different pieces of cloth joined together; a quilt or a patchwork (in the literal sense).
<ul><li><b>1995</b>, Suzanne Fisher Staples, <i>Shabanu</i>, tr. by Anneke Koning-Corveleijn, Lemniscaat (2nd ed., 1st ed. from 1991, original English from 1989), page 22.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>Af</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lappendeken.html>lappendeken</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sterren.html>sterren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verlichte.html>verlichte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lig.html>lig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:roept.html>roept</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eenzame.html>eenzame</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:herder.html>herder</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verte.html>verte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schapen.html>schapen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fluit.html>fluit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanaf.html>vanaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> top <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duin.html>duin</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Somoetimes, when I lie under the <b>quilt</b> and look at the starlit sky, a lonely herdsman calls his sheep with his flute from a dune top in the distance.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A whole consisting of many quite different parts (loosely) joined together; a patchwork (in the figurative sense).
<ul><li><b>1838</b>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:lessen.html>Lessen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> redekunst <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> fraaije <a href = vnd.unilang:letteren.html>letteren</a>, of <a href = vnd.unilang:voorschriften.html>voorschriften</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:stijl.html>stijl</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:welsprekendheid.html>welsprekendheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dichtkunst.html>dichtkunst</a>", in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gids.html>Gids</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>Vol</a>. 2, page 520. A note <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> omitted (*).

<li><b>2003</b>, F.C.L.M. ***lar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lar.html>lar</a> (60299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laizō</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laizijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to teach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">lēra</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">lēra</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lehre</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang">lār</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">lāre</b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lara.html>lara</a> (10227)</h1><br></body> 
***larch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>larch</a> (34987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From early modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Larche</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lärche</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">larche</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">larihha</i>, early borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">larix</i>, itself possibly of <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span></span> origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>larch</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">larches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A coniferous tree, of genus <i>Larix</i>, having deciduous leaves, in fascicles.
<ul><li><b>1665</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Rea_(horticulturalist)" class="extiw" title="w:John Rea (horticulturalist)">John Rea</a>, <i>Flora</i>, London: J.G. Marriott, Book III, Chapter 20, pp. 235-236,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://catalog.hathitrust.org/Record/100245605">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>The <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>Larch</a></b>-tree</i>, with us, groweth slowly, and to be found in few <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a>; it hath a rugged bark, and boughts that branch in good order, with divers small yellowish bunched eminences, set thereon at several <a href = vnd.unilang:distances.html>distances</a>, from whence tufts of many small, long, and narrow smooth leaves do yearly come forth; it beareth among the green leaves many beautiful flowers, which are of a fine crimson colour <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1716</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nicholas_Rowe_(writer)" class="extiw" title="w:Nicholas Rowe (writer)">Nicholas Rowe</a> (translator), <i>The Ninth Book of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pharsalia" class="extiw" title="w:Pharsalia"><a href = vnd.unilang:lucan.html>Lucan</a></a></i> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, <i>Miscellany Poems</i>, London: <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Tonson, Volume 6, p. 67,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/miscellanypoems06dryd">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>The Gummy <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>Larch</a></b>-Tree</i>, and the <i>Thapsos</i> there,</dd>
<dd><i>Wound-wort</i> and <i>Maiden-weed</i>, perfume the Air.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1855</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Wadsworth_Longfellow" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Wadsworth Longfellow"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Wadsworth Longfellow</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Song_of_Hiawatha" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Song of Hiawatha">The Song of Hiawatha</a></i>, Book 7,<sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Song_of_Hiawatha/Book_VII">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Thus the Birch Canoe <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> builded / In the valley, by the river, / In the bosom of the forest; / And the forest’s life <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> in it, / All its mystery and its magic, / All the lightness of the birch-tree, / All the toughness of the cedar, / All the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>larch</a></b>’s supple sinews;</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1924</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Radclyffe_Hall" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Radclyffe Hall">Radclyffe Hall</a>, <i>The Unlit <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>Lamp</a></i>, Chapter 5, Part 1,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gutenberg.net.au/ebooks07/0701131h.html">[4]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Joan <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> thinking: ‘She <a href = vnd.unilang:looks.html>looks</a> like a tree <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> it must be the green dress. But her <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> are like water, all greeny and shadowy and deep looking—a tree near a pool, that’s what she’s like, a tall tree. A beech tree? No, that’s too spready—a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>larch</a></b> tree, that’s Elizabeth; a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>larch</a></b> tree just greening <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>.'</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The wood of the <a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>larch</a>.
<ul><li><b>1916</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arthur_Ransome" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Arthur Ransome">Arthur Ransome</a>, “The Christening in the Village” in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Peter%27s_Russian_Tales" class="extiw" title="w:Old Peter | s Russian Tales">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a>’s Russian Tales</a></i>,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.gutenberg.org/files/16981/16981-h/16981-h.htm">[5]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Old <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> up early too, harnessing the little yellow horse into the old cart. The cart <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> of rough wood, without springs, like a big box fixed on long <b><a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>larch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:poles.html>poles</a> between two <a href = vnd.unilang:pairs.html>pairs</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:wheels.html>wheels</a>. The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:larch.html>larch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:poles.html>poles</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> instead of springs, bending and creaking, as the cart moved <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the forest track.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lasa.html>lasa</a> (91339)</h1><br></body> 
***lasagna.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lasagna.html>lasagna</a> (45189)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagna.html>lasagna</a></i> (and its plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagne.html>lasagne</a></i>), possibly from Vulgar Latin *<i>lasania</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lasanum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cooking <a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λάσανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lásanon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trivet or stand for a <a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Others argue the Italian <i><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagna.html>lasagna</a></i> originally derived from the Arabic (Semitic) <i>lawzinaj</i> ("almond cake").
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagna.html>lasagna</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagne.html>lasagne</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lasagnas</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagne.html>lasagne</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lasagnes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> sheet of <a href = vnd.unilang:pasta.html>pasta</a>.</li>
<li>An Italian baked dish comprising layers of such <a href = vnd.unilang:pasta.html>pasta</a> with various ingredients (usually a meat ragù (chiefly <a href = vnd.unilang:bolognese.html>Bolognese</a>), a fish ragù or a vegetarian/vegetable ragù with bechamel sauce)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In Italian, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagna.html>lasagna</a></i> refers to one <i><a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagna.html>lasagna</a></a></i> and its plural form, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagne.html>lasagne</a></i>, refers to the dish. This distinction <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rarely observed in English.</li>
<li>When the dish <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> referred to as <i><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagne.html>lasagne</a></i> (rather than <i><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagna.html>lasagna</a></i>), <i>lasagnes</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes found as the plural form, referring to multiple dishes or varieties.</li></ul>
</body>

***lass.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lass.html>lass</a> (35920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">*<a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">lōs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">loose; free; lacking; sly, deceitful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare for the short vowel Ripuarian <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Franconian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Central Franconian language">Central Franconian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr">loss</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>. The uninflected <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of this adjective develops regularly into Luxembourgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:lass.html>lass</a></i>, while the inflected <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> yields the doublet <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">lues</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slow, quiet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See the English cognate <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">loose</i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:lass.html>lass</a></strong> (<i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:lassen.html>lassen</a></b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">lasst</b>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">méi <a href = vnd.unilang:lass.html>lass</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">am lassten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>loose, unattached</li></ol>
</body>

***lassen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lassen.html>lassen</a> (20530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lasschen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to join together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Further etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unclear, but probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">lacer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tie</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***lat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lat.html>lat</a> (14822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:latte.html>latte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*latta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lattō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laþþō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lat.html>lat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:latten.html>latten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:latje.html>latje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A slate, a lath.</li>
<li>A specifically, the common shortening of <a href = vnd.unilang:meetlat.html>meetlat</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> ruler, yardstick.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a> (108)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lātan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*lātan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lētaną</i>.
</p>
